     Examples
     --------
-    >>> assertRaisesRegexp(ValueError, 'invalid literal for.*XYZ',
-    ...                                int, 'XYZ')
+    >>> assert_raises_regex(ValueError, 'invalid literal for.*XYZ', int, 'XYZ')
